In this chapter we prove that the denotational semantics is adequate,
that is, if a term M is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then M multi-step reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    ‚Ñ∞ M ‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N)  implies M ‚Äî‚Ü† ∆õ N' for some N'

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full Œ≤ reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that ‚Ñ∞ M
‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N) implies that M halts under call-by-name evaluation, which we
define with a big-step semantics written Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c, where c is a
closure (a term paired with an environment) and Œ≥' is an environment
that maps variables to closures

Recall that ‚Ñ∞ M ‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N) is equivalent to saying that Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v ‚Ü¶
v') for some v and v'.  We will show that Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v ‚Ü¶ v') implies
that M halts under call-by-name.  The proof will be an induction on
the derivation of Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v, and to strengthen the induction
hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to closures using a
_logical relation_ ùïç.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that M result in a function value to
  instead require that M result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation ùïç that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms ùîº and environments ùîæ.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥' and Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v, then ùîº v (clos M Œ≥').

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.


## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

If a value v is greater than a function, then an even greater value v'
is too.

The bottom value ‚ä• is not greater than a function.

    <a id="3273" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="3278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30796" class="Function">Funs‚àà</a> <a id="3284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3237" class="Bound">f</a>
<a id="3286" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="3290" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="3292" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="3294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3294" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3296" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3298" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="3300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3300" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3302" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3304" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3304" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="3306" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="3308" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>
    <a id="3314" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="3319" class="Bound">Œì‚äÜ‚ä•</a> <a id="3323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3304" class="Bound">m</a>
<a id="3325" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="3329" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="3331" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

If the join of two values v‚ÇÅ and v‚ÇÇ is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

On the other hand, if neither of v‚ÇÅ and v‚ÇÇ is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-‚äî"></a><a id="3979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3979" class="Function">not-AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="3994" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3996" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="3998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3998" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4001" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="4004" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4011" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="4028" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4030" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#2706" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3998" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4044" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4046" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#2706" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4001" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a>
               <a id="4075" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4077" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#2706" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4089" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3998" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚äî</a> <a id="4094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4001" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a><a id="4096" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3979" class="Function">not-AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="4113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4113" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="4117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="4121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="4130" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3458" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="4146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="4151" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4155" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4157" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4162" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4164" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4166" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="4180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4162" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4182" class="Bound">af1</a>
<a id="4186" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4190" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4192" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="4197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4197" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4199" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4201" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="4215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4197" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4217" class="Bound">af2</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-‚äî-inv"></a><a id="4363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4363" class="Function">not-AboveFun-‚äî-inv</a> <a id="4382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4384" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="4386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4386" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4389" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="4392" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4399" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4401" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4403" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#2706" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4386" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚äî</a> <a id="4420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#4389" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a><a id="4422" class="Symbol">)</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

## Big-step semantics for call-by-name lambda calculus

To better align with the denotational semantics, we shall use an
environment-passing big-step semantics. Because this is call-by-name,
an environment maps each variable to a closure, that is, to a term
paired with its environment. (Environments and closures are mutually
recursive.) We define environments and closures as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ClosEnv"></a><a id="5746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="5754" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="5764" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5766" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

<a id="5771" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Clos"></a><a id="5776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5776" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="5781" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5783" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="5787" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Clos.clos"></a><a id="5795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5795" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="5800" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5802" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="5804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5804" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="5805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5807" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5810" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="5812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5814" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5804" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="5816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="5818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="5819" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5821" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5823" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="5831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5804" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="5833" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5776" class="Datatype">Clos</a>

<a id="5841" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="5849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5849" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="5851" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5853" class="Symbol">‚àÄ</a> <a id="5855" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5856" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5858" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5849" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="5862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">‚àã</a> <a id="5864" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="5865" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5867" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5776" class="Datatype">Clos</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As usual, we have the empty environment, and we can extend an
environment.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="‚àÖ&#39;"></a><a id="5974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5974" class="Function">‚àÖ&#39;</a> <a id="5977" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="5987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">‚àÖ</a>

The following is the big-step semantics for call-by-name evaluation,
which we describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6202" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_‚ä¢_‚áì_"></a><a id="6207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6207" class="Datatype Operator">_‚ä¢_‚áì_</a> <a id="6213" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6215" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="6217" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6217" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="6218" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6220" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6217" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6232" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6234" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6217" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="6239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="6240" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6242" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5776" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6249" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6251" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6255" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="_‚ä¢_‚áì_.‚áì-var"></a><a id="6264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6264" class="InductiveConstructor">‚áì-var</a> <a id="6270"         <a id="6343" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6345" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6277" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="6347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6292" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6349" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="6351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5795" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="6356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6321" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6306" class="Bound">Œ¥</a>

       <a id="6591" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6519" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="6595" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Symbol">‚Üí</a>   <a id="6621" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6550" class="Bound">Œ¥</a> <a id="6624" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6519" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="6635" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6637" href="{%          <a id="6655" class="Comment">----------------------------------------------------</a>
       <a id="6715" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6519" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="6719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6207" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="6721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6534" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="6723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬∑</a> <a id="6725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6536" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6207" class="Datatype Operator">‚áì</a> <a id="6729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#6581" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* The (‚áì-var) rule evaluates a variable by finding the associated
  closure in the environment and then evaluating the closure.

* The (‚áì-lam) rule turns a lambda abstraction into a closure
  by packaging it up with its environment.

* The (‚áì-app) rule performs function application by first evaluating
  the term L in operator position. If that produces a closure containing
  a lambda abstraction (∆õ L'), then we evaluate the body L' in an
  environment extended with the argument M. Note that M is not
  evaluated in rule (‚áì-app) because this is call-by-name and not
  call-by-value.

If the big-step semantics says that a term M evaluates to both c and
c', then c and c' are identical. In other words, the big-step relation
is a partial function.

## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation ùïç is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction (i.e. in WHNF), whereas
the relation ùîº is for any closure. Roughly speaking, ùîº v c will hold
if, when v is greater than a function value, c evaluates to a closure
c' in WHNF and ùïç v c'. Regarding ùïç v c, it will hold when c is in
WHNF, and if v is a function, the body of c evaluates according to v.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùïç"></a><a id="8310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#8310" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="8312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="8320" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="8322" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5776" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="8327" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="8329" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="ùîº"></a><a id="8333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#8333" class="Function">ùîº</a> <a id="8335" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="8343" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="8345" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5776" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="8350" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="8352" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define ùïç as a function from values and closures to Set and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with ùîº in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then ùïç is false (Bot). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define ùïç by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9047" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="9050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#9006" class="Bound">M</a><a id="9051" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9053" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#9009" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9054" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is ‚ä•, then the result is true (‚ä§).

* If the value is a join (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of ùïç is true for both v‚ÇÅ and v‚ÇÇ.

* The important case is for a function value (v ‚Ü¶ v') and closure
  (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥). Given any closure c such that ùîº v c, if v' is
  greater than a function, then M evaluates (with Œ≥ extended with c)
  to some closure c' and we have ùïç v' c'.


The definition of ùîº is straightforward. If v is a greater than a
function, then M evaluates to a closure related to v.

id="9667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#8310" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#9611" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#9643" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). Thus, we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, ùîæ
relates Œ≥ to Œ≥' if the corresponding values and closures are related
by ùîº.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùîæ"></a><a id="10044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10044" class="Function">ùîæ</a> <a id="10046" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10048" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="10050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10050" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="10051" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10053" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#7488" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="10059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10050" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10061" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10050" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10073" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10075" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

We need a few properties of the ùïç and ùîº relations.  The first is that
a closure in the ùïç relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10490" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="10495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10495" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="10500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10502" class="Symbol">‚àÄ</a> <a id="10504" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10505" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10507" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10508" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10510" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10505" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="10516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10507" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="10518" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10520" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="10524" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.∆õ_"></a><a id="10532" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10532" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ_</a> <a id="10535" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10537" class="Symbol">‚àÄ</a> <a id="10539" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10540" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="10541" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10543" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10544" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10544" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="10546" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10548" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10540" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a> <a id="10554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="10556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="10557" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="10564" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10495" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="10571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="10574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10544" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10575" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùïç‚ÜíWHNF"></a><a id="10655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10655" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="10662" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10664" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="10666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10666" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="10667" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10669" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="10671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5746" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10666" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="10682" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10684" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="10686" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10666" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="10692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="10693" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10695" class="Bound">v</a><a id="10696" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="10705" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#8310" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="10709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10695" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10711" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5795" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10684" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="10719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10669" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="10720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10722" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10495" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="10729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10684" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="10731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10655" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="10738" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10739" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="10741" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10743" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10745" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10746" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10748" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10749" class="Bound">v</a><a id="10750" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10752" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="10755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10655" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="10762" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10763" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="10765" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="10769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10769" class="Bound">M</a><a id="10770" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10772" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10773" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10773" class="Bound">v</a><a id="10774" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10776" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10779" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10532" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ_</a>

Next we have an introduction rule for ùïç that mimics the (‚äî-intro)
rule. If both v‚ÇÅ and v‚ÇÇ are related to a closure c, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùïç‚äî-intro"></a><a id="10979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10979" class="Function">ùïç‚äî-intro</a> <a id="10988" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10990" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="10992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10992" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="10994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10994" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="10997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10997" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a><a id="10999" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="11010" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#8310" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="11014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10994" class="Bound">v‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="11017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10992" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11019" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#8310" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="11023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10997" class="Bound">v‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="11026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#10992" class="Bound">c</a>

In a moment we prove that ùïç is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if ùïç v c and v' ‚äë v, then ùïç v' c.
This property, named ùïç-sub, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the (sub) rule.

To prove ùïç-sub, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to ‚ä•. In such cases, ùïç v (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥') is trivially true.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-ùïç"></a><a id="11642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#11642" class="Function">not-AboveFun-ùïç</a> The proofs of ùïç-sub and ùîº-sub are intertwined.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-ùïç"></a><a id="12081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#12081" class="Function">sub-ùïç</a> <a id="12087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12089" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="12091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#12091" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="12093" We prove ùïç-sub by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
v' ‚äë v. We describe each case below.

    <a id="13959" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="13964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#3458" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="13975" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="13977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#13913" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="13979" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13981" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="13983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#13919" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="13986" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#13924" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="13991" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="13993" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>
<a id="13995" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="13999" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="14001" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="14006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#14006" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="14010" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14012" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">‚ä•-elim</a> <a id="14019" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14020" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="14034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#14006" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="14038" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="14042" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="14044" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="14048" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="14050" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="14055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#14055" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="14059" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14061" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">‚ä•-elim</a> <a id="14068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14069" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="14083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#14055" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="14087" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="14091" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case (Bot‚äë). We immediately have ùïç ‚ä• (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥).

* Case (ConjL‚äë).

        v‚ÇÅ' ‚äë v     v‚ÇÇ' ‚äë v
        -------------------
        (v‚ÇÅ' ‚äî v‚ÇÇ') ‚äë v

  The induction hypotheses gives us ùïç v‚ÇÅ' (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥)
  and ùïç v‚ÇÇ' (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥), which is all we need for this case. 

* Case (ConjR1‚äë).

        v' ‚äë v‚ÇÅ
        -------------
        v' ‚äë (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)

  The induction hypothesis gives us ùïç v' (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥).

* Case (ConjR2‚äë).

        v' ‚äë v‚ÇÇ
        -------------
        v' ‚äë (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us ùïç v' (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥).

* Case (Trans‚äë).

        v' ‚äë v‚ÇÇ   v‚ÇÇ ‚äë v
        -----------------
             v' ‚äë v

  The induction hypothesis for v‚ÇÇ ‚äë v gives us
  ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥). We apply the induction hypothesis
  for v' ‚äë v‚ÇÇ to conclude that ùïç v' (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥).

* Case (Dist‚äë). This case  is the most difficult. We have

        ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚Ü¶ v‚ÇÇ) (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥)
        ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚Ü¶ v‚ÇÉ) (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥)

  and need to show that 

        ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚Ü¶ (v‚ÇÇ ‚äî v‚ÇÉ)) (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥)
  
  Let c be an arbtrary closure such that ùîº v‚ÇÅ c.
  Assume (v‚ÇÇ ‚äî v‚ÇÉ) is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both v‚ÇÇ and v‚ÇÉ
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma AboveFun-‚äî,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.
  
  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì clos N Œ¥ and ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos N Œ¥).  We also have Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c‚ÇÉ and
    ùïç v‚ÇÉ c‚ÇÉ.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    c‚ÇÉ ‚â° clos N Œ¥. Also, from ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos N Œ¥) we know that N ‚â° ∆õ N'
    for some N'. We conclude that ùïç (v‚ÇÇ ‚äî v‚ÇÉ) (clos (∆õ N') Œ¥).

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say AboveFun v‚ÇÇ and ¬¨ AboveFun v‚ÇÉ. Then from ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚Ü¶ v‚ÇÇ) (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥)
    we have Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì clos N Œ≥‚ÇÅ and ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos N Œ≥‚ÇÅ). From this we have
    N ‚â° ∆õ N' for some N'. Meanwhile, from ¬¨ AboveFun v‚ÇÉ we have
    ùïç v‚ÇÉ (clos N Œ≥‚ÇÅ). We conclude that We conclude that
    ùïç (v‚ÇÇ ‚äî v‚ÇÉ) (clos (∆õ N') Œ≥‚ÇÅ).
    

The proof of sub-ùîº is direct.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#12133" class="Function">sub-ùîº</a> <a id="16165" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#5795" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="16171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16171" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="16173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16173" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="16174" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16176" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16177" class="Bound">v</a><a id="16178" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16180" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16181" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="16183" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16185" class="Bound">ùîºv</a> <a id="16188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16188" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a> <a id="16193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16193" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="16201" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="16206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16185" class="Bound">ùîºv</a> <a id="16209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#2891" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äë</a> <a id="16221" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16193" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="16225" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16188" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a><a id="16229" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="16266" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="16268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16239" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="16270" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16272" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="16274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16245" class="Bound">M‚áìc</a> <a id="16278" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#12081" class="Function">sub-ùïç</a> <a id="16286" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#16251" class="Bound">ùïçv</a> <a id="16289" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a> <a id="16294" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="16296" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

From AboveFun v' and v' ‚äë v we have AboveFun v.  Then with ùîº v c we
obtain a closure c such that Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c and ùïç v c. We conclude with an
application of sub-ùïç with v' ‚äë v to show ùïç v' c.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. In more detail, if Œ≥ ‚ä¢
M ‚Üì v and ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥', then ùîº v (clos M Œ≥'). The proof is by induction on
the derivation of Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the (var) rule.

    <a id="19217" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="19222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#17153" class="Function">‚Üì‚Üíùîº</a> <a id="19226" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19162" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="19228" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19230" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19166" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="19232" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19234" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19170" class="Bound">Œ≥&#39;</a><a id="19237" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19175" class="Bound">M</a><a id="19241" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19183" class="Bound">ùîæŒ≥Œ≥&#39;</a> <a id="19248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19201" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="19250" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19251" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#2891" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äë</a> <a id="19262" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19209" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="19266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19203" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a><a id="19270" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="19272" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="19276" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="19278" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="19280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19280" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19282" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="19284" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="19286" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19286" class="Bound">M‚áìc</a> <a id="19290" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="19292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19292" class="Bound">ùïçv</a> <a id="19295" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="19297" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="19299" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="19307" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="19309" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19280" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="19311" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="19313" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="19315" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19286" class="Bound">M‚áìc</a> <a id="19319" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="19321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#12081" class="Function">sub-ùïç</a> <a id="19327" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DenotAdequate.md %}{% raw %}#19292" class="Bound">ùïçv</a> <a id="19330" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a> <a id="19335" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="19337" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case (var). Looking up x in Œ≥' yields some closure, clos L Œ¥,
  and from ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥' we have ùîº (Œ≥ x) (clos L Œ¥). With the premise
  AboveFun (Œ≥ x), we obtain a closure c such that Œ¥ ‚ä¢ L ‚áì c
  and ùïç (Œ≥ x) c. To conclude Œ≥' ‚ä¢ ` x ‚áì c via (‚áì-var), we 
  need Œ≥' x ‚â° clos L Œ¥, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the kth-x lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case (‚Ü¶-elim). We have Œ≥ ‚ä¢ L ¬∑ M ‚Üì v.
  The induction hypothesis for Œ≥ ‚ä¢ L ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ ‚Ü¶ v
  gives us Œ≥' ‚ä¢ L ‚áì clos L' Œ¥ and ùïç v (clos L' Œ¥).
  Of course, L' ‚â° ∆õ L'' for some L''.
  By the induction hypothesis for Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ,
  we have ùîº v‚ÇÅ (clos M Œ≥').
  Together with the premise AboveFun v and ùïç v (clos L' Œ¥),
  we obtain a closure c' such that Œ¥ ‚ä¢ L'' ‚áì c' and ùïç v c'.
  We conclude that Œ≥' ‚ä¢ L ¬∑ M ‚áì c' by rule (‚áì-app).

* Case (‚Ü¶-intro). We have Œ≥ ‚ä¢ ∆õ M ‚Üì v ‚Ü¶ v'.
  We immediately have Œ≥' ‚ä¢ ∆õ M ‚áì clos (∆õ M) Œ≥' by rule (‚áì-lam).
  But we also need to prove ùïç (v ‚Ü¶ v') (clos (∆õ M) Œ≥').
  Let c by an arbitrary closure such that ùîº v c.
  Suppose v' is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that Œ≥' , c ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c' and ùïç v' c' for some c'.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for Œ≥ , v ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v'
  but we must first show that ùîæ (Œ≥ , v) (Œ≥' , c). We prove
  that by the lemma ùîæ-ext, using facts ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥' and ùîº v c.

* Case (‚ä•-intro). We have the premise AboveFun ‚ä•, but that's impossible.

* Case (‚äî-intro). We have Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) and AboveFun (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)
  and need to show Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì c and ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) c for some c.
  Again, by AboveFun-‚äî, at least one of v‚ÇÅ or v‚ÇÇ is greater than a function.

  * Suppose both v‚ÇÅ and v‚ÇÇ are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ and Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÇ
    we have Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c‚ÇÅ, ùïç v‚ÇÅ c‚ÇÅ, Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c‚ÇÇ, and ùïç v‚ÇÇ c‚ÇÇ for some c‚ÇÅ and c‚ÇÇ.
    Because ‚áì is deterministic, we have c‚ÇÇ ‚â° c‚ÇÅ.
    Then by ùïç‚äî-intro we conclude that ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) c‚ÇÅ.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose v‚ÇÅ is greater than a function
    value but v‚ÇÇ is not.  By the induction hypotheses for Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ,
    and using ùïç‚ÜíWHNF, we have Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì clos (∆õ M'') Œ≥‚ÇÅ
    and ùïç v‚ÇÅ (clos (∆õ M'') Œ≥‚ÇÅ).
    Then because v‚ÇÇ is not greater than a function, we also have
    ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos (∆õ M'') Œ≥‚ÇÅ). We conclude that ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) (clos (∆õ M'') Œ≥‚ÇÅ).
    
* Case (sub). We have Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v, v' ‚äë v, and AboveFun v'.
  We need to show that Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c and ùïç v' c for some c.
  We have AboveFun v by AboveFun-‚äë,
  so the induction hypothesis for Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v gives us a closure c
  such that Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c and ùïç v c. We conclude that ùïç v' c by sub-ùïç.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have ‚àÖ ‚ä¢ ∆õ N ‚Üì ‚ä• ‚Ü¶ ‚ä•, so ‚Ñ∞ M ‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N)
gives us ‚àÖ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì ‚ä• ‚Ü¶ ‚ä•. Then the main lemma gives us ‚àÖ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c for some c.
